<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Culture">Culture</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bitola&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Culture">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<dl>
<dt>Manaki Festival of Film and Camera</dt>
</dl>
<p>Is the oldest film festival in the world who value the work of cinematographers.In memories of the first cameramen on the Balkans, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Milton_Manaki" title="Milton Manaki">Milton Manaki</a>, every September the Film and Photo festival "Brothers Manaki" takes place. It is a combination of documentary and full-length films that are being shown. The festival is a world class event and it is a must see.Every year the festival brings world recognized actors including <a href="/wiki/Catherine_Deneuve" title="Catherine Deneuve">Catherine Deneuve</a>, <a href="/wiki/Isabelle_Huppert" title="Isabelle Huppert">Isabelle Huppert</a>, <a href="/wiki/Victoria_Abril" title="Victoria Abril">Victoria Abril</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Predrag_Manojlovic" title="Predrag Manojlovic">Predrag Manojlovic</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Michael_York_(actor)" title="Michael York (actor)">Michael York</a>, <a href="/wiki/Juliette_Binoche" title="Juliette Binoche">Juliette Binoche</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Rade_Sherbedgia" title="Rade Sherbedgia">Rade Sherbedgia</a>.</p>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Magaza_Bitola.JPG"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1224" data-file-width="1632" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f3/Magaza_Bitola.JPG/220px-Magaza_Bitola.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f3/Magaza_Bitola.JPG/330px-Magaza_Bitola.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f3/Magaza_Bitola.JPG/440px-Magaza_Bitola.JPG 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Magaza_Bitola.JPG" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
The Magaza, a gallery in the center of the city.</div>
</div>
</div>
<dl>
<dt>Ilindenski Denovi</dt>
</dl>
<p>Every year, the traditional folk festival "Ilinden Days" takes place in Bitola. It is a 4-5 day festival of music, songs, and dances that is dedicated to the Ilinden Uprising against the Turks, where the main concentration is placed on the folk culture of Macedonia. Folk dances and songs are presented with many folklore groups and organizations taking part in it.</p>
<dl>
<dt>Small Monmartre of Bitola</dt>
</dl>
<p>In the last few years, the Art manifestation "Small Monmartre of Bitola" that is organized by the art studio "Kiril and Metodij" has turned into a successful children's art festival. Children from all over the world come to express their imagination through art, creating important and priceless art that is presented in the country and around the world. "Small Monmartre of Bitola" is a winner of numerous awards and nominations.</p>
<dl>
<dt>Bitolino</dt>
</dl>
<p>Bitolino is an annual children's theater festival held in August with the Babec Theater. Every year professional children's theaters from all over the world participate in the festival. The main prize is the grand prix for best performance.</p>
<dl>
<dt>Si-Do</dt>
</dl>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Si-Do" title="Si-Do">Si-Do</a></div>
<p>Every May, Bitola hosts the international children's song festival <a href="/wiki/Si-Do" title="Si-Do">Si-Do</a>, which in recent years has gained much popularity. Children from all over Europe participate in this event which usually consists of about 20 songs. This festival is supported by ProMedia which organizes the event with a new topic each year. Many Macedonian musicians have participated in the festival including: <a href="/wiki/Next_Time" title="Next Time">Next Time</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Karolina_Goceva" title="Karolina Goceva">Karolina Goceva</a> who both represented Macedonia at the <a href="/wiki/Eurovision_Song_Contest" title="Eurovision Song Contest">Eurovision Song Contest</a>.</p>
<dl>
<dt>Festival for classical music Interfest</dt>
</dl>
<p>It is an international festival dedicated mainly to classical music where many creative and reproductive artist from all over the world take place. In addition to the classical music concerts, there are also few nights for pop-modern music, theater plays, art exhibitions, and a day for literature presentation during the event. In the last few years there have been artists from <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Slovakia" title="Slovakia">Slovakia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Poland" title="Poland">Poland</a>, and many other countries. For the reason of Bitola being called the city with most pianos, there is one night of the festival dedicated to piano competitions. One award is given for the best young piano player, and another for competitors under 30.</p>
<dl>
<dt>Akto Festival</dt>
</dl>
<p>The Akto Festival for Contemporary Arts is a regional festival. The festival includes visual arts, performing arts, music and theory of culture. The first Akto festival was held in 2006. The aim of the festival is to open the cultural frameworks of a modern society through "recomposing" and redefining them in a new context. In the past, the festival featured artists from regional countries like Slovenia, Greece or Bulgaria, but also from Germany, Italy, France and Austria.</p>
<dl>
<dt>International Monodrama Festival</dt>
</dl>
<p>Is annual festival of monodrama held in April in organization of Centre of Culture of Bitola every year many actors from all over the world come in Bitola to play monodramas.</p>
<dl>
<dt>Lokum fest</dt>
</dl>
<p>Is authentic cultural and tourist event which has existed since 2007. Founder and organizer of the festival is the Association of Citizens Center for Cultural Decontamination Bitola. The festival is held every year in mid-July in the heart of the old Turkish bazaar in Bitola, as part of Bitola Cultural Summer Bit Fest.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Education">Education</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bitola&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Education">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bitola_University" title="Bitola University">St. Clement of Ohrid University of Bitola</a> (<a href="/wiki/Macedonian_language" title="Macedonian language">Macedonian</a>: <span lang="mk">Универзитет Св</span>. Климент Охридски — Битола) was founded in 1979, as a result of dispersed processes that occurred in education in the 1970s, and increasing demand of highly skilled professionals outside the country's capital. Since 1994, it has carried the name of the Slavic educator St. <a href="/wiki/Clement_of_Ohrid" title="Clement of Ohrid">Clement of Ohrid</a>. The university has institutes in Bitola, <a href="/wiki/Ohrid" title="Ohrid">Ohrid</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Prilep" title="Prilep">Prilep</a>, and headquarters in Bitola. With its additions in education and science, it has established itself, and cooperates with <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/University_SS._Cyril_and_Methodius" title="University SS. Cyril and Methodius">University of St. Cyril and Methodius</a> from <a href="/wiki/Skopje" title="Skopje">Skopje</a> and other universities in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Balkan" title="Balkan">Balkans</a> and <a href="/wiki/Europe" title="Europe">Europe</a>. The following institutes and scientific organizations are part of the university:</p>
<div class="thumb tright">

<p>There are seven high schools in Bitola:</p>
<ul>
<li>"Josip Broz-Tito", a gymnasium</li>
<li>"Taki Daskalo", a gymnasium</li>
</ul>
<p>- Stopansko School (mining survey, part of Taki Daskalo)</p>
<ul>
<li>"Dr. Jovan Kalauzi", a medical high school</li>
<li>"Jane Sandanski", an economical high school</li>
<li>"Gjorgji Naumov", a technological high school</li>
<li>"Kuzman Šapkarev", an agricultural high school</li>
<li>"Toše Proeski", a musical high school</li>
</ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="People_from_Bitola">People from Bitola</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bitola&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: People from Bitola">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:242px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hotel_Epinal_in_Bitola.JPG"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1632" data-file-width="1224" height="320" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a1/Hotel_Epinal_in_Bitola.JPG/240px-Hotel_Epinal_in_Bitola.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a1/Hotel_Epinal_in_Bitola.JPG/360px-Hotel_Epinal_in_Bitola.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a1/Hotel_Epinal_in_Bitola.JPG/480px-Hotel_Epinal_in_Bitola.JPG 2x" width="240"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Hotel_Epinal_in_Bitola.JPG" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Hotel Epinal in the centre of Bitola, named after the <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">French</a> city of <a href="/wiki/%C3%89pinal" title="Épinal">Épinal</a>, a twin town of Bitola. In return, a quarter in the city of Épinal is called Bitola, and a <a href="/wiki/Flag_of_the_Republic_of_Macedonia" title="Flag of the Republic of Macedonia">Macedonian flag</a> is flown there.</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Further information: <a href="/wiki/List_of_people_from_Bitola" title="List of people from Bitola">List of people from Bitola</a></div>
<p>Some notable people born in Bitola are:</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ajri_Demirovski" title="Ajri Demirovski">Ajri Demirovski</a> (Macedonian: Ајри Демировски, Turkish: Hayri Önder) (born 1927 in Bitola (Monastiri), died 2009 in Turkey) was an ethnic Turkish singer.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Karolina_Go%C4%8Deva" title="Karolina Gočeva">Karolina Gočeva</a>, pop singer</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Dimitar_Ilievski-Murato" title="Dimitar Ilievski-Murato">Dimitar Ilievski-Murato</a>, first Macedonian to climb Mount Everest</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Miljan_Miljani%C4%87" title="Miljan Miljanić">Miljan Miljanić</a>, football coach</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nikol%C4%8De_Noveski" title="Nikolče Noveski">Nikolče Noveski</a>, footballer</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Georgi_Sugarev" title="Georgi Sugarev">Georgi Sugarev</a>, IMRO revolutionary</li>
</ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Twin_towns_.E2.80.94_Sister_cities">Twin towns — Sister cities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bitola&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Twin towns — Sister cities">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">See also: <a href="/wiki/List_of_twin_towns_and_sister_cities_in_Macedonia" title="List of twin towns and sister cities in Macedonia">List of twin towns and sister cities in Macedonia</a></div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="References">References</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bitola&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: References">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="reflist columns references-column-count references-column-count-2" style="-moz-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2; column-count: 2; list-style-type: decimal;">
<ol class="references">
<li id="cite_note-1"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-1">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a class="external text" href="http://www.vecer.com.mk/?ItemID=CD3D6FA9DF1BE245B5CF81C6E1721E1C" rel="nofollow">www.vecer.com.mk</a> Saint Nectarios of Bitola proclaimed new city patron. (26-01-2008) <span class="languageicon" style="font-size:0.95em; font-weight:bold; color:#555;">(Macedonian)</span></span></li>

<li id="cite_note-15"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-15">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">"There was a large "Greek" population, both in town and country, but of these a very large proportion were Vlachs, many were South CHAPTER EIGHT 68Albanians, others were Slavs. Few probably were genuine Greeks. But they belonged to the Greek branch of the Orthodox Church, and were reckoned Greek in the census."</span></li>
